    <p class="mt-3">DCS has an enchanting physical environment spread over an area of 1500 sq.m, with state of
        the art
        laboratories to support the M.Tech programmes, research laboratories, air-conditioned Conference room
        and Auditorium, well organised library, class rooms, faculty rooms, office et cetra. Apart from the
        wi-fi hotspot in the department, all its constituents are provided with access points to the wired
        net.</p>

                                                <div class="mm1-com mm1-admi-com mm1-s1">
                                                <h4>Academic Programmes</h4>

<p>CUSAT is academically structured into 9 faculties: Engineering, Environmental Studies, Humanities, Law, Marine Sciences, Medical Sciences & Technology, Science, Social Sciences and Technology.

</p><p>CUSAT has at present 27 Departments of study and research offering Graduate and Post Graduate programmes across a wide spectrum of disciplines in frontier areas of engineering, science, technology, humanities, law & management.

</p><p>Centres in specialized thematic areas have been established by the University, to encourage and promote collaborative, multi-disciplinary interaction. Conceived as umbrella organizations for inter-faculty interaction and joint enterprises, aimed at wholesome integration, assimilation and dissemination of knowledge beyond all sectarian confines, these Centres are expected to engage themselves in unfettered intellectual pursuits.

      }

        background-repeat: no-repeat;}
      .cube__face--right  { background: #fff; }

        background-repeat: no-repeat; }

      .cube__face--bottom { background: #ff006f; }

      .cube__face--right  { transform: rotateY( 90deg) translateZ(50px); }
      .cube__face--back   { transform: rotateY(180deg) translateZ(50px); }
      .cube__face--left   { transform: rotateY(-90deg) translateZ(50px); }
      .cube__face--top    { transform: rotateX( 90deg) translateZ(50px); }

      <script>
      var cube = document.querySelector('.cube');
      var currentClass = '';
      var i=1;
      function changeSide(r) {
      showClass = 'show-'+r;
        if ( currentClass ) {
          cube.classList.remove( currentClass );
        }
      //alert(r)
      //alert(currentClass);
       // cube.classList.add( showClass );
       // currentClass = showClass;
      }
      
      
      window.setInterval(function(){
      s = i%6;
      //alert(s);
      i++;
      if(s==1){
       changeSide("top");
      }else if(s==2){
       changeSide("front");
      }else if(s==3){
        changeSide("left");
      }else if(s==4){
       changeSide("right");
      }else if(s==5){
        changeSide( "back");
      }else if(s==0){
       changeSide("bottom");
      }
      }, 2000);
      
      </script>
      <script type="text/javascript">
    //Change Found
var $affectedElements = $("body,div p, span ,h4,p,ho-ev-link span, .con-title h2 span,.con-title h2,.course-overlay span,.wed-foot-link ul li a ,.wed-hom-footer h4,.col-md-3,col-md-3 h4,h2,h1, h4,about-sp p, .cor .about-sp .stu-life-cond p,.stu-life p, body p,.stu-life-cond p"  ); // Can be extended, ex. $("div, p, span.someClass")

// Storing the original size in a data attribute so size can be reset
$affectedElements.each( function(){
  var $this = $(this);
  $this.data("orig-size", $this.css("font-size") );
});

$("#btn-increase").click(function(){
  changeFontSize(1);
})

$("#btn-decrease").click(function(){
  changeFontSize(-1);
})

$("#btn-orig").click(function(){
  $affectedElements.each( function(){
        var $this = $(this);
        $this.css( "font-size" , $this.data("orig-size") );
   });
})

function changeFontSize(direction){
    $affectedElements.each( function(){

        var $this = $(this);
        //alert($this.css( "font-size"));

        $this.css( "font-size" , parseInt($this.css("font-size"))+direction );
    });
}

</script>

		function viewOD($sid) {
		$("#loaderIcon").show();
			jQuery.ajax({
				url: "view_kforum.php",
				data:'id='+$sid,
				type: "POST",
				success:function(data){
					//console.log(data);
					$("#display").html(data);
					$("#loaderIcon").hide();
					},
				error:function (){}
				});
		}	
        </script>

	<div class="mkdf-eh-item-inner">

			<div class="mkdf-row-grid-section-wrapper " ><div class="mkdf-row-grid-section"><div class="vc_row wpb_row vc_inner vc_row-fluid" ><div class="wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-12 vc_col-lg-6"><div class="vc_column-inner vc_custom_1496665541535"><div class="wpb_wrapper"><div class="mkdf-section-title-holder  mkdf-st-standard mkdf-st-title-left mkdf-st-normal-space mkdf-st-disable-title-break" style="text-align: left">
	<div class="mkdf-st-inner">
					<h2 class="mkdf-st-title" >
				Unleash the Entrepreneur<br /> in You!			</h2>
							<p class="mkdf-st-text" style="font-size: 17px">
				CITTIC CUSAT provide a springboard to budding entrepreneurs who wish to launch themselves into the world of technology based business careers. In CITTIC, bright ideas can be developed to a product or service using advanced technology solutions. This innovation centre is designed to provide all the support to make business ventures successful.			</p>
			</div>

				Incubation Space			</h2>
							<p class="mkdf-st-text" style="font-size: 17px">
				CITTIC offers both physical and virtual incubation. CITTIC provide workspace with shared office facilities with emphasis on business and professional services necessary for nurturing and supporting early stage growth of technology and technology based enterprises. Common pool of hard and soft infrastructure like meeting/conference room, teleconferencing facilities, library etc.
If interested to incubate at CITTIC send request along with one page of your idea/product to cittic@cusat.ac.in			</p>

<!-- Header Image  -->
<div class='inside-header-image d-flex align-items-center p-3' style='background-image: linear-gradient(rgba(23, 24, 69, 0.7), rgba(23, 24, 69, 0.7)), url("assets/images/header-images/header-phd.jpg")'><div class='header-text-container text-center'><h3 data-aos='fade-up'>Ph.D</h3><h5 class='dcs-breadcrumbs-text' data-aos='fade-up' data-aos-delay='100'><a class='dcs-breadcrumbs' href='index.php'>Home</a> &gt; Admission &gt; Ph.D</h5></div></div><!-- End Header Image  -->
<!-- Text Container -->
<div class='container p-3 mt-4'>

    <p class="mt-3">The Department of Computer Science came into existence in 1984 with an M.Tech. course in Computer and Information Science,
    which was the first in Kerala. The department currently offers full-time and part-time M.Tech programs
    in various specializations, a five-year integrated M.Sc. course, and Ph.D. programs in the areas of Artificial Intelligence, 
    Computer Vision, Natural Language Processing, Cyber-Physical Systems, Bioinformatics, and Software Engineering. The Department collaborates
     through MoUs with academic and industrial partners including the University of Glasgow, TCS, UST Global, ITC, and Infenox Technologies.
      Additionally, the department is also involved in collaborative research with foreign universities like the Research Council of Norway, 
      NTU Singapore, Queen's University UK, and Indian institutes including IISc. , various IITs, IIITs, and NITs. 
      The department has 8.75 Cr worth of ongoing consultancy and funded projects including the INTPART Project (NTNU Norway), SPARC Project, 
      and RUSA Project(Govt. of India). Department faculty has received teaching and research awards including AICTE Visvesvaraya Best 
      Teacher Award (2021), Kairali Research Award (2020), Distinguished Young Faculty Award (2020), and 
      DRDO Academy Excellence Award (2020). In 2024, CUSAT was ranked in 801+  Computer Science subject-wise category by THE World University Rankings.
      The department also is entrusted with the responsibility of managing the upcoming High Performance Computing facility worth 26 Cr. 
      The department also provides technical expertise and support to various Government/Quasi-government bodies




    </p>
    <h6 class="blue-bold-heading mt-3">Core Areas of Research</h6>
    <p class="mt-2">Natural Language Processing, Theoretical Computer Science, Distributed Computing, Information
        Systems Engineering, Computer Networks, Mobile Computing</p>

    <!-- Alumni Page Content -->
    <p class="mt-3">
        We are in the process of collecting and updating the alumni details of the Department of Computer Science,
        CUSAT. By doing so we hope to provide a meeting place for all previous and current students of the department
        whereby they can know each other better and share their knowledge. Also upon getting in touch with enough
        alumnus we intend to create a strong and active alumni asscociation for the department.
        <br><br>
        If you were a student of this department, please send a mail to <a href="mailto:dcsalumni@cusat.ac.in"
                                                                           class="text-link">dcsalumni@cusat.ac.in</a>
        giving your email id (will be used for login), name, batch, programme, present address and phone no., current
        profile etc. Please send a scanned passport size photo(preferably color) of yours as well.Your details including
        your photo will be accesible only to the alumnus upon login and not to the public.
